## 19. I talk, I walk



<table border=1 style='margin: auto; word-wrap: break-word;'><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>I talk Kittens mew Doves coo Birds cheap Chicks peep Lions growl Dogs howl Monkeys chatter Starlings clatter Ducks quack Hens clack Parakeets squawk But I talk - Magdalen Eichert</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>I walk Frogs jump Caterpillars hump Worms wriggle Bugs jiggle Rabbits hop Horses clop Snakes slide Seagulls glide Mice creep Deer leap Puppies bounce Kittens pounce Lions stalk But I walk - Evelyn Beyer</td></tr></table>

##### Language

1.  $ \underline{\text{Doing words}} $

Doing words are called 'verbs'

1. Make the sounds in the poem 'I talk'.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c1b49d25-a7d1-4fe7-bb16-190a820e77a1/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_59_1496_130_1615.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A43Z%2F-1%2F%2Fa04cd591b6e1320952c2a12e974031d2c45ccb74a3c6f204bcb2ddf39e0e1021" alt="Image" width="5%" /></div>


2. Act out the actions in the poem 'I walk'.

3. Combine and act out a pair of sounds and actions of your choice.

Example: bounce and coo; creep and howl

## 2.  $ \underline{\text{Read, think and say}} $

look at these examples with your class.

Example:

Do-doing - did

Say-saying - said

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c1b49d25-a7d1-4fe7-bb16-190a820e77a1/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_334_542_698_911.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A44Z%2F-1%2F%2F247b00243de135e45531f812628dad93224341a55343329848975e8e89b35beb" alt="Image" width="30%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c1b49d25-a7d1-4fe7-bb16-190a820e77a1/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_745_432_1051_882.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A44Z%2F-1%2F%2F3ed174f1e44674c13823143d94fbc44b9926bcdeeafc899713a8cf5e95de2354" alt="Image" width="25%" /></div>


Help the class do the same with the given words

Dig, draw, drink, fall, feel

Fight, grow, hear, hide, hit

Hold, let, lose, read, ride

Ring, sleep, tear, write, win

Wore, wake

##### Revision of sounds

Make one word using each ending given in the box.

Do not use the words given in the poems above.

#### ALL ABOUT ME

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//42f8838e-30f7-4685-ad25-5c7dc3d92d5e/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_32_207_174_364.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A44Z%2F-1%2F%2Ff262a3dd9d4c6849298efa93044601b8825e3f56e4a4d76402a0d7b38cc64a16" alt="Image" width="11%" /></div>


Hello friends! You all know about me. Who are you? Tell me something about yourself.

An identity card has all information about us, like our name, address and guardian's phone numbers. An identity card tells others who we are. It is very important for our safety and we should wear it to school every day.

3. Fill in the blanks with what you do not like and also choose the reason.

a.I do not like dirt on  $ \underline{\text{A}} $r  $ \underline{\text{mit}} $  $ \underline{\text{a}} $r  $ \underline{\text{ku}} $k $ \underline{\text{n}} $a because.

○ it looks bad.

○ it smells bad.

○ it makes air and water bad.

b. I do not like to eat  $ \underline{\text{Pomegranate}} $ because,

✓ I do not like how it tastes.

○ I do not like how it looks.

○ I do not like how it smells.

c. I do not like to wear  $ \underline{\text{jeans}} $ because,

✓ I do not like how it looks.

○ I do not feel comfortable in it.

○ I do not like how it looks, but for a change I can wear it someday.

##### MY DIFFERENT MOODS

I am happy, when I come to school.

Then, I dance with joy.

I am sad, when I cannot go out to play.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//2f511758-51c3-4e55-b061-69046e2b3a5a/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_522_1215_737_1402.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2F1ba2d5299f04e6acedd7f1224a66bf21cc3b817c1f76c6b2792359b2ed5ab77e" alt="Image" width="18%" /></div>


Then, I enjoy playing an indoor game.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//2f511758-51c3-4e55-b061-69046e2b3a5a/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_0_1448_153_1612.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2F04ce47ee223ca398f60e23432304a0fadc458043ca07a1b80302ffef1603c945" alt="Image" width="12%" /></div>


I feel scared, when clouds thunder.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//2f511758-51c3-4e55-b061-69046e2b3a5a/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_568_1400_724_1622.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2F6d3e7075a4d4176910d2b5d426e4a6482835dfff1bede21466e86d290e35c520" alt="Image" width="13%" /></div>


Then, I count from 1 to 10 and I calm down.

Then, I clap and jump with joy.

##### Let us recite this poem.

When I am happy, I laugh and smile.

When I am sad, I sit and cry.

When I am angry, I stamp my feet.

When I am scared, I take a deep breath.

When I am tired, I go to sleep.

In any way, what I feel, I can show it to you.

Do you, also ever feel the same way like I do?

##### WORD MASTER

information-fact

sick-unwell

mood-feeling

angry-displeasure

scared-afraid, fearful

dessert-sweet dish

excited-thrilled

unique-being the only of its kind, special

#### LIFE SKILL- MANAGING EMOTIONS

What is your choice? Tick the correct option.

When, I am angry I choose to-

○ throw the things around me.

clench my teeth.

○ yell and cry.

☐ not talk to anyone.

Other things, I choose to do.

Making wrong choices, when I am sad or angry is not good for myself and others should take a deep breath and think calmly. The things, I do are (colour the boxes your choice).

Take a deep breath and count up to 20.

Talk to myself about it.

Read a book.

Drink some water.

Think of my favourite things.

Talk to someone about it.

Think about what made me angry.

Another thing that I like to do to calm myself-

Draw what mad

me angry.

### FUN WITH FRIENDS

Make a 'Managing My Mood Box', using paper carton. Fill the box with items that help you to calm down and cheer up. These could be colouring books, and crayons, perfumes that smell good or pictures of your favourite things. Think, what all will you put inside the mood box?

##### THE STORY OF OUR FIVE SENSES

I am the best of all the body parts. People can see the beautiful world around them with my help.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//7f9cc31b-d539-4ec0-901a-ac7fe732b66c/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_225_895_494_1123.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A53Z%2F-1%2F%2Fdaec1dd242b94ae362bbc3889ea28fa901883b92061c56a1ea94b8cfa1eb59a3" alt="Image" width="22%" /></div>


No, I am the best body part. People hear sounds with my help.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//7f9cc31b-d539-4ec0-901a-ac7fe732b66c/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_662_823_966_1116.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A53Z%2F-1%2F%2F5ddb1d1f3eb62df9cc64f22d4a4fd787c31f101521895a3163b62fff1363dcbe" alt="Image" width="25%" /></div>


Stop it, you both. I help people to smell. They are able to breathe because of me.

You all are wrong, I help people to feel the things. They can tell or feel whether a thing is hot or cold, smooth or rough, because of me. So, I am the most useful body part for them.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//7f9cc31b-d539-4ec0-901a-ac7fe732b66c/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_326_1146_638_1459.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A53Z%2F-1%2F%2Fb931eee199ee1e69558a2fb95b7dce1ca30887ee3103e3bcbd51b6d5f724a1f9" alt="Image" width="26%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//7f9cc31b-d539-4ec0-901a-ac7fe732b66c/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_648_1142_888_1382.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A53Z%2F-1%2F%2F1109eef30ca65aee0a6beeb8417979b6f83f85378cb3ffdea89b8361e72224aa" alt="Image" width="20%" /></div>


Tongue

I help them to taste and speak. We should put it like this - all five of us, together help people to feel the world. That is why, together we are called 'The Five Senses'.

Sense organs make the world so bright and clear.

How wonderful it is to see, feel, smell, taste and hear!

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//7f9cc31b-d539-4ec0-901a-ac7fe732b66c/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_488_49_558_127.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A53Z%2F-1%2F%2Ff769ff75d8554346429628a40a5a85fa03f6a65050ada346b6d442d210ddabc3" alt="Image" width="5%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//7f9cc31b-d539-4ec0-901a-ac7fe732b66c/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_155_138_235_251.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A53Z%2F-1%2F%2F0dee8fe73b0a766548786b8c9963b30a9e62c0d16b7800eb2020c1ad6c7f45b6" alt="Image" width="6%" /></div>


##### WISDOM BOX

Our tongue has taste buds that help us identify or feel different tastes like-sweet, salty, sour and bitter.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//7f9cc31b-d539-4ec0-901a-ac7fe732b66c/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_1023_117_1141_288.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A53Z%2F-1%2F%2F12c28cf365ca0f63d79e87c01e6d188fb02859057f0d6a1a6d65f8c67f305328" alt="Image" width="9%" /></div>

TAKING CARE OF OUR BODY PARTS

We must keep our body parts clean to stay healthy.

##### We must-

brush our teeth in the morning, when we wake up and at night before going to bed.

- wash our hands with soap and water before and after eating our meals, after coughing or sneezing and after using the toilet.

• rinse our mouth thoroughly with water after every meal.

• bathe daily with soap and clean water. Then, we must wipe ourselves dry with a clean towel.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//7f9cc31b-d539-4ec0-901a-ac7fe732b66c/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_767_991_941_1230.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A54Z%2F-1%2F%2Fb77c2d575926b743397b05963a50b14db27b0163f215378001ddded724e18911" alt="Image" width="14%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//7f9cc31b-d539-4ec0-901a-ac7fe732b66c/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_994_992_1144_1241.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A54Z%2F-1%2F%2F90ede0efa8bf1a20a980054ea44fe9be24a4a66e3edfb7e168bee72a28ad1a14" alt="Image" width="12%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//7f9cc31b-d539-4ec0-901a-ac7fe732b66c/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_778_1263_946_1521.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A54Z%2F-1%2F%2F6990991436770fddc8880c997f3f225bc14e4c23eaaf4871337b88f3579138bd" alt="Image" width="14%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//7f9cc31b-d539-4ec0-901a-ac7fe732b66c/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_974_1267_1143_1517.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A54Z%2F-1%2F%2Fbf7c0029f6c95e3a271df3bd0d0935ff67ac24dc63a5d3d1a5162e09aa55d021" alt="Image" width="14%" /></div>


wash our hair with shampoo regularly and comb our hair everyday.

trim our nails regularly.

exercise daily. It keeps us fit. Playing outdoor games, running, cycling and swimming are some good exercises.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fa23df76-1e80-4651-b7d1-8a3fb0618ba5/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_676_73_881_292.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A43Z%2F-1%2F%2F880001ade9695b27940a2d64542da004ee97203c81783d02f94a521fb9137844" alt="Image" width="17%" /></div>

Games-

Indoor games can be played inside a building.

Outdoor games are played outside, in an open space.

Classify the games here as indoor or outdoor games. Write 'I' for indoor games and 'O' for outdoor games.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fa23df76-1e80-4651-b7d1-8a3fb0618ba5/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_6_706_146_853.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A43Z%2F-1%2F%2F7c811aacd9beb48962aa99b39260f3f7317e6664b60a91c9275ae118702a9c45" alt="Image" width="11%" /></div>

##### WISDOM BOX

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fa23df76-1e80-4651-b7d1-8a3fb0618ba5/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_26_1158_120_1277.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A44Z%2F-1%2F%2F9d1c438e55e1388406cfdf936c75f86588e5d74a5f397b139eaab95303a746e0" alt="Image" width="7%" /></div>


Breathing deeply anytime during the day helps us to stay healthy.

Being active is important, so is getting some rest. We may get tired after a long day of study, play and chores. We must get eight hours of sleep daily.

If we do not get enough rest, we may fall sick.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fa23df76-1e80-4651-b7d1-8a3fb0618ba5/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_695_1253_1133_1598.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A44Z%2F-1%2F%2F36459502bec7c311f14c3b3e4db010c526a6392b23b81d05d31f38fe5724a0c0" alt="Image" width="36%" /></div>


We must follow these good habits to stay healthy.

• Eat healthy food and drink plenty of water.

• Do yoga and simple breathing exercises every day.

• Cover our mouth with a handkerchief while sneezing and coughing.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fa23df76-1e80-4651-b7d1-8a3fb0618ba5/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_795_20_1053_280.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A44Z%2F-1%2F%2F7724d79fb69467963614436795ed4bd97127f3a2a4cd718e9c66ea352656989d" alt="Image" width="21%" /></div>


- Cover our nose and mouth with a mask in case we have cough and cold.

• Stay happy and wear a smile on our face always.

• Avoid eating uncovered food.

• Wear mask in crowded places.

• Avoid touching our face.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fa23df76-1e80-4651-b7d1-8a3fb0618ba5/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_814_319_965_670.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2F5d482ceee4c35118927f5e487b04fe33b7f519fe5681370313f31d64cb37355e" alt="Image" width="12%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fa23df76-1e80-4651-b7d1-8a3fb0618ba5/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_974_223_1157_493.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2Fbeaed2d9614f56a987011cb7c15070dba9b91de7071400ab8905223c82d66e42" alt="Image" width="15%" /></div>


##### PEOPLE WITH SPECIAL NEEDS AROUND US

Not everyone is able to use their body in the same way like others can.

##### Let us meet Disha and Tom.

I am Disha. I cannot walk. But, I can move and do other work while being seated in my wheel chair.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fa23df76-1e80-4651-b7d1-8a3fb0618ba5/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_450_870_652_1115.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2F35afe445dabbae213d5410d2ecad5f0dc71ef08f2ef2ed13272a7adaedf9279d" alt="Image" width="16%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fa23df76-1e80-4651-b7d1-8a3fb0618ba5/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_678_807_904_1115.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2F42f24b08f19ce0cd5d71fee20280d0ad3cc7e4e4438c916703e62ca7098902de" alt="Image" width="18%" /></div>


I am Tom. I cannot see, but my other senses are very strong. By touching and smelling, I can feel things.

We should help and respect everyone around us.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fa23df76-1e80-4651-b7d1-8a3fb0618ba5/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_476_1183_542_1259.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2Fb7142250400a2503bdd95b7ccc5ec8ce7ffaa74af31adc01af33840a173c71e3" alt="Image" width="5%" /></div>


##### WISDOM BOX

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fa23df76-1e80-4651-b7d1-8a3fb0618ba5/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_145_1320_200_1406.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2Ffe20cbadfa714715a944708e2f8279a9748a2557f2dcf09e6d65a26af1ab093f" alt="Image" width="4%" /></div>


Do you know that we can read by the sense of touch?

Braille is a system that enables blind people to read and write by touching. Braille was invented by Louis Braille. It follows a pattern like-

A $\bullet$ R $\bullet\bullet$ r $\bullet$

The Indian 10 rupee coin has ten raised marks to assist us in identifying the currency by the touch sense.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fa23df76-1e80-4651-b7d1-8a3fb0618ba5/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_351_1378_432_1412.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2F10e02c31e0ea1464c927f90aba3d1ddf651965908c538497297380a8643b3680" alt="Image" width="6%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fa23df76-1e80-4651-b7d1-8a3fb0618ba5/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_1039_1354_1150_1490.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2Fc0f0035ac8556b5c1812b3ad25e4cadfea00d40fcc55c959c11c2f5f0cb798fa" alt="Image" width="9%" /></div>


### FUN WITH FRIENDS

Make a simple sensory script like Braille, using paper and a pointed pencil. Close your eyes and feel how a person, who cannot see, can read with the help of a sensory script.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fa23df76-1e80-4651-b7d1-8a3fb0618ba5/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_850_131_1097_277.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2Fc1dddaad1ce55586a9cbe3315ce871d01b5a2848ed7689356499f9b2a81a66f5" alt="Image" width="20%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fa23df76-1e80-4651-b7d1-8a3fb0618ba5/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_22_315_95_388.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2Ff7f09f724c467a63b049ddcf7cd54252594257cb6499fdce2a7d866d6e909fdf" alt="Image" width="6%" /></div>


##### WORD MASTER

taste buds- the parts of the tongue which help us to identify, feel different tastes bitter- having a sharp taste rinse- wash with clean water trim- cut neatly chores- daily routine

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fa23df76-1e80-4651-b7d1-8a3fb0618ba5/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_23_584_88_660.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2Fe10060bdbeef122e9d95bd4d7b47427787e6e35026e415a419647b90c003e76d" alt="Image" width="5%" /></div>


##### LET'S TRY

### A. Choose the correct option.

1. Our ears help us to _____.

○ see ○ hear ○ talk

2.We smell food with our_____

☐ hands ☐ nose ☐ ears

3. While taking a bath, we should use ___.

○ soap and water ○ a tooth brush ○ a handkerchief

4. Which one of the following activity is done using hands?

☐ holding a ball ☐ running ☐ chewing our food

### B. Write true or false.

1. Breathing exercises keep us healthy.

2. We should not drink enough water.

3. Taste buds help us to taste only sweets.

4. We clean our teeth with a toothbrush.

# TYPES OF FAMILIES

We live together in a family. We love and help each other in a family. All families are not the same. Some families are small, while some are big. Let us different types of families.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//72f82221-0ba1-4752-97c5-913959e87d8b/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_117_290_375_704.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2F8c68e602d6f2d6df5753f395951c66296768f4357dd5a2c9259306e382c2b545" alt="Image" width="21%" /></div>


I am Zoya. This is my family. My father, mother, brother and I live together. We are a small family.

My friend Rishi lives with his mother only. They are a single-parent family. His family is also a small family.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//72f82221-0ba1-4752-97c5-913959e87d8b/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_822_241_1023_606.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2Faff594eb3852ff84c92d70f570660f1cf7a710acd95f981bc5792802c1e8cb64" alt="Image" width="16%" /></div>


My uncle, aunt and cousins live with my grandparents. They are a big family.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//72f82221-0ba1-4752-97c5-913959e87d8b/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_1062_312_1166_747.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2F1d6bca0e18ade01de8eb063c3c879cbe4e6e1be29f131642a690791f886c5bd8" alt="Image" width="8%" /></div>

##### WISDOM BOX

Single-parent families have one parent, either a mother or a father. The parent takes care of the child/children.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//72f82221-0ba1-4752-97c5-913959e87d8b/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_142_1021_354_1384.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2F19c3a0275636cafa450d857833476512c17bd7e2b5add2ca8fe1df691390c257" alt="Image" width="17%" /></div>


My neighbours have a pet. It is a dog. They take good care of their dog. The dog is a part of their family.

##### FAMILY FUN

Our home is the first place of learning. We learn a lot of things from our family members. They help us in growing up as a good person. Most of the members of a family share a common last name after the first name called surname.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//72f82221-0ba1-4752-97c5-913959e87d8b/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_7_345_72_427.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2F9c2cfe1334ba8bc0abadb89109376ba2af8f1d0740d876b8671fac0b6ff9e0ad" alt="Image" width="5%" /></div>

CELEBRATIONS IN A FAMILY

Family members celebrate happy occasions together. They celebrate birthdays, weddings and housewarming parties together.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//72f82221-0ba1-4752-97c5-913959e87d8b/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_97_627_410_944.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2F5c049183e8a288d016eee6e37fa5aec3652ae2d21b1b94cc9b884eb920a940a7" alt="Image" width="26%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//72f82221-0ba1-4752-97c5-913959e87d8b/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_814_482_1159_801.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2F939fa5471978cd73b8f496fbbc99161461328ffd4116f713971f5b1e31e513e4" alt="Image" width="28%" /></div>


They also celebrate festivals together. Festivals are special days. These are the times to have fun, meet people and share food. Festivals help us to understand our culture. They also help us to spread love and bring people closer.

Bharat is a land of festivals. We celebrate festivals like- Holi, Dussehra, Diwali, Eir Christmas and Gurpurab. We also celebrate harvest festivals like- Pongal, Onam ar Baisakhi.

Sometimes, family members visit places of worship to celebrate festivals.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//72f82221-0ba1-4752-97c5-913959e87d8b/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_197_1125_366_1325.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2Fad4a67de25a91b029730c2baffb7bdcca8b314db24eefb37ff88a3de0d81bb01" alt="Image" width="14%" /></div>

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//72f82221-0ba1-4752-97c5-913959e87d8b/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_446_1137_635_1326.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2F130300cc3b8cd1f3f15738e00118e935861ff1e8b52003c4de0a9e9a16e8444f" alt="Image" width="15%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//72f82221-0ba1-4752-97c5-913959e87d8b/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_124_1334_286_1483.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2Feef38fb7e046eb2a178cd63b66b2f4a7d1cec5ec0184664a5a1aecf3ea944122" alt="Image" width="13%" /></div>

##### WORD MASTER



<table border=1 style='margin: auto; word-wrap: break-word;'><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>surname-the last name</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>relative- a person connected in family</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>sorrows-unhappiness</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>housewarming- a celebration for moving in a new house</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>occasion-event</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>culture-way of life</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>ship-pray</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>grocery- house hold and food items</td></tr></table>

##### LET'S TRY

### A. Choose the correct option.

1. We live at home with our _____.

○ friends ○ family ○ neighbours

2. A family with only the mother and a child is a _____.

○ big family ○ small family ○ single-parent family

3. Members of a family ___.

☐ cook together ☐ share work ☐ cook together and share

4. ___ is a place for worship.

○ Mosque ○ Onam ○ Holi

B. Tick the correct words in the given sentences.

1. We live with our family/friends.

2. Members of a family share/do not share their happiness together.

3. Gurudwara is a festival/place for worship.

4. All families are same/different.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//6a8a1e3b-e113-4c51-88cb-5f6e68c0163f/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_134_1073_219_1155.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A44Z%2F-1%2F%2F675d036b8468af56f524fb307a611ff97b932b6f4828400d00a5719e81e334b7" alt="Image" width="7%" /></div>

D. Write the full name of any four of your classmates. Underline their surnames with red colour and their first names with green colour.

IMPORTANCE OF A HOUSE

A house keeps us

safe from heat and

cold.

safe from rain and storm.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//bbd3ee48-23fa-4141-b896-570157dfbf76/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_310_772_1113_1360.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2Fffa41596d602653af84c0365519d3a5ef471708d778fcd9e5d7a2c575a94ef63" alt="Image" width="67%" /></div>


safe from thieves.

safe from wild animals.

safe from germs and some diseases.

Like us, animals also need a house or a place to live in. A house protects animals from bad weather, hunters and other animals. It also protects them from accidents.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//bbd3ee48-23fa-4141-b896-570157dfbf76/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_13_117_68_225.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2F1231a5a7c89d5de3a364865a39c47458f2cf5d7ac93fb8047ae17df65bde2a52" alt="Image" width="4%" /></div>

##### TYPES OF HOUSES

Pucca house is a house made of cement, bricks, iron, steel, concrete and wood. These houses are strong and long lasting. Single or multi-storey buildings and bungalows are pucca houses.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//bbd3ee48-23fa-4141-b896-570157dfbf76/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_806_608_1097_912.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2Fdaf9a33d8ad12b4047c445d820cc1328dbbad40d07f6530f628b00e9f661c1ff" alt="Image" width="24%" /></div>

Multi-storey building

Bungalow

Wood and mud hut

Kutcha house is a house made of wood, straw, bamboo, mud and dry leaves. These houses are not very strong. A mud hut is a kutcha house.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//bbd3ee48-23fa-4141-b896-570157dfbf76/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_336_1376_405_1457.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2F0fdbd9e877c1146d7ab4781031d232feecbe676018e216ef40f20ca50dff6a50" alt="Image" width="5%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//bbd3ee48-23fa-4141-b896-570157dfbf76/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_28_1445_92_1557.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2F1354fe3efb79c1a7afcf8ded3b3704eaff38df2f5926f91edf83f6ecdc8c7dc0" alt="Image" width="5%" /></div>


##### WISDOM BOX

There are many people who help us in building our house, like- mason, carpenter, plumber, electrician and painter. We should respect them for their help.

Diana wants to build a bungalow and a hut. Circle the things, she will need to build a bungalow. Tick the things, that she can use to build a hut. Make a star above the things that she can use to build both types of houses.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//bbd3ee48-23fa-4141-b896-570157dfbf76/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_114_69_1166_594.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2Ff2242672c2ce295959e93091459d8858f81fcb11494d881af40c2a3dfd67c363" alt="Image" width="88%" /></div>


##### PUCCA HOUSE

A pucca house has many doors and windows. We enter our house through the mo door. Windows bring in sunlight and fresh air.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//bbd3ee48-23fa-4141-b896-570157dfbf76/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_216_724_1125_1129.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2Fa9dc4bf9a98e87b559a1b546d52ce3c8fdcfbdc79a08546215c4b64658795bdb" alt="Image" width="76%" /></div>


The roof, covers the top of a house. Hot places have houses with flat roofs. Places heavy rains and snowfall have houses with sloping roofs. This is to allow rain water or snow to drain off easily.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//bbd3ee48-23fa-4141-b896-570157dfbf76/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_243_1256_604_1550.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2Ff09f21fa23985b76d0fe521cbc50b80609c0a97dc2c95963fb205ee064589bbc" alt="Image" width="30%" /></div>


Flat roof

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//bbd3ee48-23fa-4141-b896-570157dfbf76/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_731_1296_1127_1556.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2F8160416f27037656b93461d208c0d9e66aa4ae906a9f61352fd1f96e19c6dd1e" alt="Image" width="33%" /></div>


Sloping roof

Floor is the bottom surface of a room.

Walls are made of bricks or stone. They enclose or divide a room. A wall supports water pipes and electric wirings.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//bbd3ee48-23fa-4141-b896-570157dfbf76/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_749_93_1078_240.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2Fe307f321260507b6e3c56ce070d45b7cb81b0e65b6556448225b102391bfdae5" alt="Image" width="27%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//bbd3ee48-23fa-4141-b896-570157dfbf76/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_41_200_251_456.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2F6bf26d8eb057dd47f6f762f0a687dbfcd24c43ef6f4baae8bb46ad83aecb00d0" alt="Image" width="17%" /></div>


Water pipeline and electric wiring

Grills

Some houses have grills. These are made of steel and iron.

##### WISDOM BOX

Walls, windows and doors of our houses are painted to protect them from the harmful effects of water and sun.

Oh! My house is so untidy, I wish it was neat and clean.

### A HEALTHY HOUSE

We will together help you clean your house.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//bbd3ee48-23fa-4141-b896-570157dfbf76/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_269_683_874_1112.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2Fc1c93942703aa74145de057b57477886589a54720e52c0deeae8fc540b7dc0de" alt="Image" width="50%" /></div>


Thank you, for your help.

It is important to keep our house clean. A neat and clean house is a healthy house. A healthy house should-

• be free from insects and pests, such as flies, mosquitoes and rats.

have many doors and windows to allow enough sunlight and fresh air inside.

have a proper drainage system for dirty water to flow out.

have two separate dustbins for dry and wet waste.

· have things kept at their proper place.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//bbd3ee48-23fa-4141-b896-570157dfbf76/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_621_1189_1162_1574.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2F78ce5ae36b9a9e19066ffb664ac0080b724b72f021566d9f6d19928866565743" alt="Image" width="45%" /></div>


# SAFETY IN YOUR HOUSE

Who are you?

What are you doing at my home?

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//bbd3ee48-23fa-4141-b896-570157dfbf76/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_394_127_622_429.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A49Z%2F-1%2F%2F8a097016613468dbad9e53ed57b2207d282ba41258d5a48c1005415e6142b51d" alt="Image" width="19%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//bbd3ee48-23fa-4141-b896-570157dfbf76/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_652_146_896_397.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A49Z%2F-1%2F%2F2a286cb968069a0fdd10274035be6e02801ff5e0416c01a3d226e08b4b704add" alt="Image" width="20%" /></div>


• Ask an elder when you want to use sharp objects like scissors, knives and blades.

• Stay away from gas stove, fire and matchsticks.

- Avoid touching any electrical item with wet hands and bare feet. You can get an electric shock.

• Take medicines only from your parents.

• Avoid jumping on a bed or a sofa as you can fall and hurt yourself.

• Be careful when you are standing in the balcony or on the terrace.

• If someone makes you feel uneasy in your house, walk away and tell your parents or somebody you trust.

I am danger.

I am present everywhere.

To keep me away, you need to follow house safety rules.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//bbd3ee48-23fa-4141-b896-570157dfbf76/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_876_408_1152_1204.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A49Z%2F-1%2F%2Fb11ea11eb2973f7332c93b62fcefba32643cd5a44c30ce45ace77771cc291236" alt="Image" width="23%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//bbd3ee48-23fa-4141-b896-570157dfbf76/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_146_1172_233_1240.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A49Z%2F-1%2F%2Fb94b24d1240ed82f9cb667db2c29e257106c191db401bf3ad7915a3291b11289" alt="Image" width="7%" /></div>


##### WORD MASTER

kennel-a dog's house

germs- tiny living things that

make you sick

accident- harm

drain off-remove

disease-sickness

enclose-to surround

hunter-one who kills animals for food or sport

concrete-stones used for making house

uneasy-not comfortable

##### LIFE SKILL - RESPECTING OTHERS

We should respect and welcome our guests.

What should you do, if your relatives visit your house? Tick the correct option.

Greet them with a smile.

Offer water to them.

○ Do not talk to them.

Medical Room- Students, teachers and other staff go to this room, if they feel unwell. There is a nurse in the medical room to attend them.

Office- Parents pay fees in the office. Records of students are kept here.

loya got tired of looking for her bag. She went to use the toilet. She met her friend there.

Have you seen my school bag?

In the classroom, Joya saw many things.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d593610e-59ee-457d-afb2-1bf697a3072d/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_210_77_1092_738.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A44Z%2F-1%2F%2Fcb81ca18ecabd2bd0e87b2b2ff141df6d13874dd42a9ab2fb00755462f41d679" alt="Image" width="74%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d593610e-59ee-457d-afb2-1bf697a3072d/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_143_708_300_841.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2F3df13251a132deeefa528544e4ad8828199671dbdf0f8c62061ac3486fd2fe78" alt="Image" width="13%" /></div>


Can you name the objects circled in the picture above? Can you find Joya's school bag in the classroom?

Finally, Joya got her bag and she sat in the classroom to study. It was her favourite EVS class. She was ready to learn from her teacher.

##### WISDOM BOX

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d593610e-59ee-457d-afb2-1bf697a3072d/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_163_1311_271_1444.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2F9f4787bdd37003de4254c8cac0e84a912ea21c5a8604365e13dbff85d80c4157" alt="Image" width="9%" /></div>

# GOOD CHOICES AT SCHOOL

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d593610e-59ee-457d-afb2-1bf697a3072d/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_325_116_644_347.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2F7b83450dd8ffd3d73c39fecbe715fba2009c2e8e987c0c8495d2920602896af2" alt="Image" width="26%" /></div>


We must follow good choices at our school.

• Wear clean and ironed uniform.

• Reach school on time.

• Listen to your teachers say.

• Be kind to your classmates.

• Use the dustbin for throwing waste.

• Respect people who help us at school.

• Keep your school clean.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d593610e-59ee-457d-afb2-1bf697a3072d/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_838_219_1098_527.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2Fb990026b064284929b7a21c8e792f265d494f231fc47459774c3f9b456310d1e" alt="Image" width="21%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d593610e-59ee-457d-afb2-1bf697a3072d/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_667_515_983_808.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2F03e5f9effff124134cbd3b4424749d61b4c6bae9bef2ef795243a4b447e0165f" alt="Image" width="26%" /></div>

SAFETY RULES TO BE FOLLOWED AT SCHOOL

Hey, Danger! What are you doing in my school?

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d593610e-59ee-457d-afb2-1bf697a3072d/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_416_892_559_1104.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2Fc613d2e2aec297e610abc1a88c1505c5f688a43ca0df85cdda211d8d7981f08b" alt="Image" width="12%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d593610e-59ee-457d-afb2-1bf697a3072d/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_626_928_810_1108.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2F2b4a63eafd85f6a3ad348568a414833ccd4a8b9f9c737f5649cb3a2c13e5710c" alt="Image" width="15%" /></div>


• Keep your bottle and bag at a proper place.

• Respect school property like desks and chairs.

• Wait patiently when standing in a line.

• Walk carefully on the stairs.

• Stand in a queue while waiting for the school bus.

• Always get in or out of the vehicle after it has stopped.

• Remain seated in a moving vehicle.

• Beware of strangers in and around school.

I want to alert you. You should be safe at school too.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d593610e-59ee-457d-afb2-1bf697a3072d/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_850_1072_1178_1364.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2F259bccace6bd061906f6eac88a4ed943e6d314f7a1377508f03ae9feb56dd5a1" alt="Image" width="27%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d593610e-59ee-457d-afb2-1bf697a3072d/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_829_1372_1179_1617.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2Fb9836271987f2f6b718313c41bc93c4d8e4417b4e82eafb099e36f2168b406bc" alt="Image" width="29%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c4f1f590-8740-45ab-aa79-561b9857eb91/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_39_57_116_131.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2F8df01703b6aa10e283d45887fbae08167c2b3594bb7043727a3bde25dd2132e0" alt="Image" width="6%" /></div>


##### WORD MASTER

gather-come together

auditorium-a room to perform dance, play, song or other activities

littering-make untidy

classmates- member of the same class in a school

stranger-unknown person

##### LET'S LEARN

### C. Choose the correct option.

1. The helper, generally not seen in school is ___.

TYPES OF PLANTS

There are different kinds of plants around us. Some plants are big while some are small.

Big plants- Trees are big and strong plants. They have thick and woody stems called trunks. Banyan tree, mango tree and coconut tree are some examples.

Bean plant

Creepers- Creepers are plants with very weak stems. They grow along the ground. Bottle gourd, watermelon and pumpkin plants are creepers.

#### PLANTS - OUR GREEN FRIENDS

plants are helpful to us in many ways.

plants-

give us clean and fresh air to breathe.

give us shade and shelter.

, are home to many birds and animals.

, give us variety of food.

, give us wood, paper, rubber, oil and medicines.

##### TAKING CARE OF PLANTS

water them regularly.

keep the plants at a sunny place.

Plants need a lot of care.

Weshould-

'not pluck parts of the plants or hurt them.

'not cut trees for our own benefits.

##### WISDOM BOX

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//0e7785f8-4923-46ed-89ab-241cb9642956/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_123_116_205_228.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A49Z%2F-1%2F%2Fdf9fddef81780451873f6abeca2a24a83df8eec29f952a373c8502f84790246b" alt="Image" width="6%" /></div>


Long back, women from a village of Uttar Pradesh hugged the trees and stood by them to stop officials cutting them down. This act of hugging, standing with trees was named as the CHIPKO Movement. As a result many trees were saved from being axed.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//0e7785f8-4923-46ed-89ab-241cb9642956/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_1047_86_1163_268.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A49Z%2F-1%2F%2F37b1e5a7cd18f0891c9e9bcc9fcb3cdeb9977161a95944f1b00e7e09629c4252" alt="Image" width="9%" /></div>

3. It has many branches that grow close to the ground.

F. Think and answer.

Can you sit under the shade of a herb or a shrub? Give reasons for your answer.

Let us hang this bird feeder. Birds must be hungry and thirsty.

Animals are living things, found everywhere on earth. There are different types of animals such as insects, birds and reptiles. They need air, food, water and shelter to live.

Different animals, live in different places.

Some animals like dogs, deer and camels live on land.

Animals like monkeys and birds live on trees.

##### WISDOM BOX

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//3e014c2d-d400-44c6-90e9-bf427ac7049a/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_130_1368_207_1485.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A44Z%2F-1%2F%2F832382d437114ed7b7d3aea91837f008f69a68555d4979a7b5a12b5f2cf67d7b" alt="Image" width="6%" /></div>


Polar bears live in very cold places covered with snow and ice. They swim in ice cold water and hunt fish to eat.

Animals are our true friends. They help us in many ways. Animals that stay in our house are called pet animals. Cows and dogs are the most common pet animals.

#### We should take care of our pets by-

· giving them fresh food and clean water.

· taking them out for walks.

• keeping them clean.

· not teasing them.

· taking them to the vet when they fall sick.

· giving them love and affection.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//3e014c2d-d400-44c6-90e9-bf427ac7049a/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_615_271_1134_681.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2Fe4674cb8ddbb8a7b1d6d28fb8e264a276eae28b85d6b00f11d88ed3bfe4302c3" alt="Image" width="43%" /></div>

##### WISDOM BOX

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//3e014c2d-d400-44c6-90e9-bf427ac7049a/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_35_787_110_904.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2F9764b29c6092ef1b856b27b19f9da60655e1ac9e3351b7fa2066ca1716e997ee" alt="Image" width="6%" /></div>


Some animals work for us. Horses and camels are used for transportation. Police dogs help the police to find thieves. It is cruel to use animals for our ease. We should be kind to them.

##### WHAT DO ANIMALS EAT?

Animals such as cows, sheep, goats, horses and deer eat grass and leaves.

Animals such as lions, leopards, polar bears, hyenas and cheetahs eat other animals.

Some animals such as bears, squirrels, rats and crows eat both plants and animals.

##### TYPES OF ANIMALS

Birds- We see many birds flying in the sky. Birds are animals that have wings and feathers. Most birds can fly. Birds eat with their beaks. They do not have teeth. They have two legs.

##### WORD MASTER

hungry-need for food

vet-one who treats sick or hurt animals

thirsty-dry, water less

ease-comfort and peace

affection-love and care

scales- flat pieces on the skin of fish and snakes

##### LET'S LEARN

### C. Choose the correct answer.

1. Identify the animals that eat only leaves and grass.

○ Deer and cow ○ Crow and bear ○ Lion and cheetah

2. A _____ is not an insect.

    ○ mosquito ○ housefly ○ sparrow

3. What is common among a woodpecker, an owl and a monkey?

○ They are animals. ○ They live on trees. ○ Both of these.

4. Snakes, crocodiles, alligators and lizards are ___.

birds ☐ insects ☐ reptiles

giving it fresh/stale food.

## 2 years

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c00ce193-efe7-4ff7-8fc0-c5876a450b5b/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_443_1233_625_1442.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2Fd1ccb9113268a79a28a06f13aa116f99a732b9df2db825ab00eab2d29ed25a0d" alt="Image" width="15%" /></div>


4 years

Aarav loves drinking milk. Aarav loves to eat porridge.

Aarav enjoys eating a variety of foods.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c00ce193-efe7-4ff7-8fc0-c5876a450b5b/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_804_1241_1085_1427.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2F648a2613d2a79a95bdb00230844f438c4307fdbd6da58daf7ffdfcd14dcb9edf" alt="Image" width="23%" /></div>


All of us need food. It helps us to live and grow. It also gives us energy to work and play.

We eat different food items to remain healthy and strong.

Generally, we eat three meals in a day.

We have our breakfast in the morning, lunch in the afternoon and dinner at night. We also have snacks in between our meals. We should have healthy food items as snacks.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c00ce193-efe7-4ff7-8fc0-c5876a450b5b/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_681_4_1172_469.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2Fb7e2afc8cf98cba4df3194dba2955e74c345fbab420ab37af9af7aa728d8fb9f" alt="Image" width="41%" /></div>


Snacks

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c00ce193-efe7-4ff7-8fc0-c5876a450b5b/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_60_422_224_566.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2F4e970890852bfb7da0d7bc00b03353830b556d5ed5083320447d8e18210de81f" alt="Image" width="13%" /></div>

##### SOURCES OF FOOD

We get our food from plants and animals.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c00ce193-efe7-4ff7-8fc0-c5876a450b5b/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_64_1099_1146_1562.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2F4d34c32247241519003aa465a3b97afeb4178caaf45607bab352b74115cac17f" alt="Image" width="90%" /></div>


Food from plants

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c00ce193-efe7-4ff7-8fc0-c5876a450b5b/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_7_1541_95_1616.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2F757d67bc8798386230eac7414926bcb842a2a3b8e1f438e92d3ab3bd66c2b2b0" alt="Image" width="7%" /></div>


Food from animals

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c00ce193-efe7-4ff7-8fc0-c5876a450b5b/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_796_1626_845_1665.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2F4975d7b907f2bec4052b493130b34f3fc337cc879e0645f16aadb5186deb587e" alt="Image" width="4%" /></div>


We can decide, what we want to eat. Some food choices are

Vegetarian

Food from plants, milk

and its products are called

vegetarian food.

Non-Vegetarian

Food items like chicken,

meat, egg and fish are

called non-vegetarian

food.

Vegan

Food only from plants are

called vegan food.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c00ce193-efe7-4ff7-8fc0-c5876a450b5b/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_22_301_318_490.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A50Z%2F-1%2F%2F633a2a46b75faf729c549d62fe1e64bfd2d23df7a2a55996cc95be8d79481235" alt="Image" width="24%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c00ce193-efe7-4ff7-8fc0-c5876a450b5b/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_391_315_738_471.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A50Z%2F-1%2F%2Fb5eb8328fbdc89705c388a31ed7a7e4831f2e85f9e02a47283745cf40d0688e7" alt="Image" width="29%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c00ce193-efe7-4ff7-8fc0-c5876a450b5b/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_813_293_1100_494.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A50Z%2F-1%2F%2F67e3e8397df0f7d69f6ae2df4b5f76b8def1e631dd19800f4109f47651c80756" alt="Image" width="24%" /></div>


We should respect the food choices of a person.

##### WHAT DO WE DRINK?

We drink water to live.

We must drink 6-8 glasses of clean water daily to remain healthy. Drinking water should be stored in a clean and covered vessel.

Some of the other things that we drink are milk, fruit juices, coconut water and soups.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c00ce193-efe7-4ff7-8fc0-c5876a450b5b/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_787_1181_1131_1615.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A50Z%2F-1%2F%2F632dc2b2ac7a5f5b9f2d7bca7ff968b19fe13370a6131f1128e80f2461d618ed" alt="Image" width="28%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c00ce193-efe7-4ff7-8fc0-c5876a450b5b/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_797_1626_843_1663.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A50Z%2F-1%2F%2Fdc9c8bdf1faf1299d281a8eb8183a4b755259ef40a21ead5b2dd547943ef4304" alt="Image" width="3%" /></div>


# HEALTHY FOOD HABITS

##### We must-

• eat the three meals at fixed times of the day.

• never miss a meal.

• eat a variety of local and seasonal foods.

• eat freshly cooked food.

• take small bites.

· chew our food well with our mouth closed.

• avoid eating uncovered food.

• wash our hands before and after eating.

• drink lots of water.

• rinse our mouth after every meal.

• never waste food.

I avoid eating junk food as they are not healthy.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//ca37aebe-a7ad-43ac-8cd0-1687f6047a36/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_78_876_326_1039.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A44Z%2F-1%2F%2F5a58edbf6dd7863d35bbd9906aaf37476f6dff168f10a83edec3aa00864898e5" alt="Image" width="20%" /></div>

We eat some food in raw form and some in cooked form. Cooking makes food soft and easy to digest. It also makes the food tasty and good to smell.

#### LIFE SKILL- EATING HEALTHY

FUN WITH FRIENDS

#### THE CLOTHES WE WEAR

Rearrange the given letters to name these clothes.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//0eab2eb0-54a1-4ba5-a404-37e311c2efdb/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_783_667_903_754.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2F905f1a7d93c9db3c69a8d249ed9ab50dd9ae335d1d7334a70bbf7658b6021c4e" alt="Image" width="7%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//0eab2eb0-54a1-4ba5-a404-37e311c2efdb/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_778_376_903_531.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2F43df7e7e1d8f195484af37c77c7f282012b98456d77a8f5b49527a2021ae5812" alt="Image" width="7%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//0eab2eb0-54a1-4ba5-a404-37e311c2efdb/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_767_911_913_1041.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2F9a24a462c63bf690763b6e2d8737e081827ab1b44b4f9be935128b1383f14164" alt="Image" width="8%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//0eab2eb0-54a1-4ba5-a404-37e311c2efdb/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_96_0_272_138.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2Fae5645f04585cfb6a3317d4b20edad6b74c07db50e5e2f161cdc7fafc1a846f6" alt="Image" width="10%" /></div>


Curtain

We wear clothes to cover and protect our body from heat, cold, wind, rain, sun, dirt, dust and insect bites.

Cloth is also used to make things like bags, bedsheets, curtains, sofa covers and carpets.

##### CLOTHES FOR DIFFERENT SEASONS

In summer, when it is very hot, we must wear cotton clothes to keep ourselves cool and dry. We get cotton from the cotton plant

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//0eab2eb0-54a1-4ba5-a404-37e311c2efdb/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_444_2_802_255.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2F51412aa7dea96afaea00adc62819d4824214fb85a28c8a6009afa4af7896c6ad" alt="Image" width="21%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//0eab2eb0-54a1-4ba5-a404-37e311c2efdb/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_648_862_924_1042.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2F450425580923ff71e604de95d8825123a90c68fac5870181184f45adf4d2bbab" alt="Image" width="16%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//0eab2eb0-54a1-4ba5-a404-37e311c2efdb/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_706_444_906_587.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A49Z%2F-1%2F%2F73c1831063b3be682b5924374a614ecf6b51996c1a7c6cfafee9bd96b6c8b0c5" alt="Image" width="11%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//0eab2eb0-54a1-4ba5-a404-37e311c2efdb/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_817_4_1239_401.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A49Z%2F-1%2F%2Fdecebd50990089458fc5cbe895da65bc8a8bc77efdf13dbd87603c38b078340c" alt="Image" width="25%" /></div>


In winter, when it is very cold, we must wear woollen clothes. These clothes protect us from the cold weather and keep us warm. We get wool from sheep, goat and yak.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//0eab2eb0-54a1-4ba5-a404-37e311c2efdb/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_1147_662_1316_918.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A49Z%2F-1%2F%2Fe7585ab01313cdf164b986d5e181bf91577b607b1ca35e74691f9aaa53553521" alt="Image" width="10%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//0eab2eb0-54a1-4ba5-a404-37e311c2efdb/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_1423_14_1628_1134.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A49Z%2F-1%2F%2F0c961207488de472a3b06edb63caf3806f83a6480e5740cd70bb774e638b9354" alt="Image" width="12%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//0eab2eb0-54a1-4ba5-a404-37e311c2efdb/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_141_122_574_472.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A49Z%2F-1%2F%2Fd280f00a18d6f9e1abc010bb4b836a220c514372f58f2e90b53739dc762486fe" alt="Image" width="25%" /></div>


In rainy or monsoon season when it rains, we must wear raincoats and waterproof footwear to keep ourselves dry. We must also use umbrellas so that we do not get wet in the rain.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//0eab2eb0-54a1-4ba5-a404-37e311c2efdb/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_349_625_491_776.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A49Z%2F-1%2F%2Fe39b8dc7da3bd7ced56964af51ab95777f08accbbc9b04020aebeb3a9954aba1" alt="Image" width="8%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//0eab2eb0-54a1-4ba5-a404-37e311c2efdb/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_338_902_476_1048.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A49Z%2F-1%2F%2Fba92d93a0f8ee1a758ad38823958db2c6731d2a7a542da5b965a31d8736c926e" alt="Image" width="8%" /></div>


Take a piece of cotton cloth, a woollen cloth and a piece of plastic. One by one, place each one of them on your hand and place water drop over it. What did you observe? Which of them did not wet your hand? In the same way, in rainy season, cloth made of plastic protects us from rain.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//0eab2eb0-54a1-4ba5-a404-37e311c2efdb/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_1009_694_1067_1096.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A50Z%2F-1%2F%2F9e79de7b336abcb665b68becb4204e7fa89e5d08ac9cac118dc3e1e164d4b277" alt="Image" width="3%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//0eab2eb0-54a1-4ba5-a404-37e311c2efdb/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_849_60_983_219.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A50Z%2F-1%2F%2Fc6b4c6632530c95d98a835526d01e80ef85743b7a1859decbb0aa72b0deb5b03" alt="Image" width="7%" /></div>


Make a 〇 for the correct sentences and a ▲ for the wrong sentences.

Wewear

Kimono is worn in Japan.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//caf16474-ab9e-4f07-b291-4f4d58ff7683/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_802_20_1582_1099.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2F02f2c955039bb6d5f0e91c39d2b9eccf4d7a531efb15af04475f081a6a82ff84" alt="Image" width="46%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//caf16474-ab9e-4f07-b291-4f4d58ff7683/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_371_476_649_577.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A45Z%2F-1%2F%2F6ec98e730897701e6ed49d2fbf903c1102f36d804d07ada6473a02e8939b8c9a" alt="Image" width="16%" /></div>


Saree is mainly worn in Bharat, Sri Lanka, Pakistan, Bangladesh and Nepal.

<div style="text-align: center;"><div style="text-align: center;">People in different parts of the world wear different types of clothes. A particular type of dress is called a costume. Let us see costumes from some places around the world. Generally these costumes are worn for important occasions.</div> </div>

I love wearing a variety of clothes.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//caf16474-ab9e-4f07-b291-4f4d58ff7683/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_978_41_1314_500.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2F5249d5b7abb9a4a270646cf73a5c67843e0dc819d7d6a21e9f4e850b45a3f44f" alt="Image" width="19%" /></div>


I wear special clothes on special occasions like- festivals, weddings and birthday parties. Such clothes are also called party wear clothes.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//caf16474-ab9e-4f07-b291-4f4d58ff7683/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_1256_826_1516_917.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2F35021b7a55108aa8368714f059e908859ac62f63fd34a9ed4e4f638aa453fabf" alt="Image" width="15%" /></div>


At home, I prefer to wear clothes like-T-shirts, shorts, kurtas or pyjamas.

We should wear clean and well ironed clothes. Dirty clothes can make us sick. We should take care of our clothes.

Get dressed

Sequence the steps to be followed to wear a T-shirt. Step 1 is marked for your help.

Pull the bottom of the T-shirt over the belly.

Look for the back side of the T-shirt.

Pick up the T-shirt by the bottom.

Put your right arm into the right sleeve.

Put your left arm into the left sleeve.

Put your head through the T-shirt.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//7c1ceb2d-aced-4cd6-b1d5-dbd349ad2e1f/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_926_5_1225_1027.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2Fe66c07e1388a595ad92b197fa775162fb90e1a6310a9bd1f0361b70ead61f461" alt="Image" width="17%" /></div>


Self-help is the best help. We should learn to do things on our own. This will help us in becoming independent children.

Organise a fancy dress party in your class. Each child should wear a dress representing a specific region of our country. They can also wear uniforms of people who do different jobs.

A tree in a storm

Moving air is called wind.

A very soft wind is called a breeze.

A very strong wind is called a storm.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//7c1ceb2d-aced-4cd6-b1d5-dbd349ad2e1f/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_627_616_710_684.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2Fe45efbbbdcce151842385a79b4e7a4d1dc915e776ad2ba89a654dbe3a1747418" alt="Image" width="4%" /></div>

Sometimes when you cycle or run fast, your hair sway all around you. This happens because your body moves through the air.

This change in the shape of the balloon is because of the air filled inside it. After that, prick a needle in it and see the air escaping from it. Notice the change in the shape of the balloon. NWID ___

EEBRZE

Air is used by plants to make their food.

• Air is filled into footballs, balloons, swimming tubes and culetures

and cycle tyres.

Air helps to dry clothes.

Air helps things to burn. It helps in cooking our food.

• Wind makes kites and parachutes fly.

• Wind allows boats to sail.

##### SOURCES OF WATER

A. Fill in the blanks with correct words from the brackets.

1. Very soft wind is called a ___. (breeze/storm)

2. Air is used by plants to make their ___. (food/house)

3.Dust, smoke and germs make the air ___ (dirty/clean)

4. Water is home to animals like ___. (cow/fish)

B. Choose the correct option.

☐ plants

○ animals

2. Wind helps ___ to fly.

both of these

○ drink and bathe ○ cook and wash clothes ○ wash utensils

Hello, I am Tina. Roma, Aarav and Paul are my friends. Our houses are close to one another. We are neighbours. We like to play games together. Our neighbours and places around our house together form the neighbourhood. Let us read this story about my neighbourhood.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//b6ee86ba-ca96-4d47-aeaf-176edee2c9a8/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_710_1026_1021_1119.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2F0795e78d7edaa6ddf46e6d2f3a7f3247a3ca27005e2d59db63ead60b845e37d2" alt="Image" width="18%" /></div>


Sam uncle did not like talking much with others in our neighbourhood. He always scolded us for making noise while playing. All children used to dislike him.

One fine evening, a child fell while playing. Sam uncle helped him by giving him first aid. From that day, we all realised that he is a good person. He is now a good friend of ours.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//b6ee86ba-ca96-4d47-aeaf-176edee2c9a8/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_514_2_906_528.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2F659512080fb6a0d2c9272eb5ab840446d2069f025cb928cae18e65a8e7de52f7" alt="Image" width="23%" /></div>


We should respect all kind of people.

be respectful to our neighbours.

It is important to be a good neighbour. To be a good nei

we should.

help each other when needed.

• share each other's joys and problems.

celebrate festivals and special occasions together.

• spend time together.

greet everyone with a smile.

• invite them home sometimes.

##### Market

Hospital is a place where doctors and nurses treat us when we fall sick. A hospital also has office staff to help us. An ambulance is used by hospitals to carry sick people.

There are many shops in the market to buy food items, fruits, vegetables and milk. There are also cloth shops, eateries, salons and gadget shops around.

##### Temple

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fadff716-ac89-4d78-a16c-e9382c326139/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_1294_819_1452_1002.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2F36cc647fff79327d6ba88034c5a582b766b0e4f1a8054ce76082892be09c7727" alt="Image" width="9%" /></div>


We get petrol and diesel for our vehicles from the fuel station.

Bus stop is the place from where we board a bus. We can travel to various places in the city and from one city to another city on a bus.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fadff716-ac89-4d78-a16c-e9382c326139/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_1067_557_1233_734.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2Fab25dec627e0abf0c13b70e70735ab559f5d17cf0072c8ae5afc67a16d7e1cf7" alt="Image" width="9%" /></div>


##### Police station

Railway station

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fadff716-ac89-4d78-a16c-e9382c326139/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_1253_474_1497_669.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2Fee4ffec56bdfec44bfd48b941536d3ec91e5fbb67bc3b61a4568872ef4debaae" alt="Image" width="14%" /></div>


Gurudwara Church

We go to places of worship to offer prayers

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fadff716-ac89-4d78-a16c-e9382c326139/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_732_1024_1007_1120.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2F2d12a3145a0743a3838c64f0c922bff239ce56b90eff5096429c2a4fc4fad87d" alt="Image" width="16%" /></div>


Police station is a place where the police work to guard. They travel in a police gyp or on a bike. They keep a neighbourhood safe from thieves, pickpockets and others.

We go to the railway station to board trains to travel from one city to another.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fadff716-ac89-4d78-a16c-e9382c326139/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_693_0_839_283.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2Fbb56177a5404593d88fbe48c8f3d51401554ad212e75fc4f660f7623e3f6104e" alt="Image" width="8%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fadff716-ac89-4d78-a16c-e9382c326139/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_1201_225_1404_449.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2F4390175297c71bb4e6dd7bec33d8d222b9397c52ee08d69dadab3ebd6b595b3b" alt="Image" width="12%" /></div>


School and College

Bank is the place where we safely keep our money and valuable things. There are ATMs in our neighbourhood. ATMs are Automated Teller Machines. We use ATMs to take out our money.

We learn many things a school and college with the help of our teachers.

Wow! My neighbourhood has both essential and non-essential services

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fadff716-ac89-4d78-a16c-e9382c326139/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_209_1014_391_1101.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2F0ca8269820a200bc40fabbb6290a65d6c1a536f2b8dc33caf9cc388594d91b83" alt="Image" width="10%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fadff716-ac89-4d78-a16c-e9382c326139/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_374_101_622_561.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2F99cfba4e88a3e3a1a7943f6f18d0b082c6eeb1b1d74545c664d85336df3b74cb" alt="Image" width="14%" /></div>


At last, Biju saw the park. There were trees, benches and swings in the park. He saw children and elders playing, walking and relaxing in the park.

Essential services are the services that we need even during a crisis. These include services like chemists, hospitals, police services, groceries and banks. Rest of the shops and services come under non-essential services.

• keep our neighbourhood clean.
