### There are many people who help us keep our neighbourhood clean like house helps, garbage collectors and many more. We should respect them and be thankful to them.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fadff716-ac89-4d78-a16c-e9382c326139/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_407_780_640_1024.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2Fadf3a3744a776e6c7b089776cad673cb0a2df8ddf6278e63b5722414bfdd2f22" alt="Image" width="13%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fadff716-ac89-4d78-a16c-e9382c326139/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_352_400_621_676.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2F804789d7e086011e19cca2997fa53282158c62bae898639e06e148f123fae227" alt="Image" width="15%" /></div>


I am here to alert you. You should be aware of strangers in and around your neighbourhood.

Being safe in your neighbourhood

• Talk to strangers only in presence of your family

• Whenever a stranger approaches you and offers a ride or a candy or a toy, step away and yell "No!"

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fadff716-ac89-4d78-a16c-e9382c326139/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_755_1019_1017_1119.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2F7b9633352ea899c033ca383c2aa861ca3a4adbc2d5f03a3370a4816f11114434" alt="Image" width="15%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fadff716-ac89-4d78-a16c-e9382c326139/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_618_0_1181_325.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2Fd7d11ed5e0430b2ff2504033c8a770aa535a9c9b89d64b5fcd84083fdf083861" alt="Image" width="33%" /></div>


• If you get lost, look for a person in uniform, like a police officer or security guard for help. If there are no people in uniform, look for people with their family they may be able to help you.

• Never share your house address and phone numbers with any stranger.

##### WORD MASTER

First aid-first medical help given before a doctor

essential-needed, must

approach- to come or go near to

A scientist finds new things and studies about them in detail.

##### OUR NATIONAL SYMBOLS

Our national symbols are symbols of our freedom and unity. Our National Flag is the symbol of pride and patriotism.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c17914f2-b0b6-4c95-94a1-cf69313c1ef0/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_121_249_451_549.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2F3d1cc10fd3c6b4f478f5df10ede62619655740d316789ff2812acd45f20bcacb" alt="Image" width="27%" /></div>


Deep saffron- power and bravery of our country

White- truth, purity and peace

Navy blue Ashok Chakra- growth

Green-wealth and life

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c17914f2-b0b6-4c95-94a1-cf69313c1ef0/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_253_594_418_922.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2F6214dcc7fb27eced8ffdcc4eb307eeb8217c71505dd52a76fa3eee32e48ece17" alt="Image" width="13%" /></div>


Our National Emblem is the seal of our country. We can see it on our notes and coins.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c17914f2-b0b6-4c95-94a1-cf69313c1ef0/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_185_1131_556_1409.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2F6606e22fcbec44bce562362188f9168b2778289c1715dbf42cc8fc6be84ac0a2" alt="Image" width="31%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c17914f2-b0b6-4c95-94a1-cf69313c1ef0/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_737_729_1152_828.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2Fb2da46a181755d2d8c20ddee64a128231bbe18760441e8f28ead04c596e5341b" alt="Image" width="34%" /></div>


Our National Animal is Tiger. It shows strength and power.

Our National Anthem is Jana-gana mana. It is sung on all important occasions like- Republic Day and Independence Day.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c17914f2-b0b6-4c95-94a1-cf69313c1ef0/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_773_1138_1133_1400.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A46Z%2F-1%2F%2F126e17e4b973f09d03e55b20cd1e4ac083923287d7b5d01701a100321a36ce7c" alt="Image" width="30%" /></div>


Our National Bird is Peacock. It is a symbol of peace and grace.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c17914f2-b0b6-4c95-94a1-cf69313c1ef0/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_32_163_117_314.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2F3ac54156d9658e56029eaa96188c268f8a5bde9f37c28e704d7f5bebc6d2ebd8" alt="Image" width="7%" /></div>

#### CHANGING FACE OF BIRTH

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c17914f2-b0b6-4c95-94a1-cf69313c1ef0/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_365_69_524_252.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A50Z%2F-1%2F%2F70a6a509edbb49f0d3f5a642f1d1a0400902f8223602cd703612090cf8c1b000" alt="Image" width="13%" /></div>


Long ago

I have been seeing Bharat for many years now. Life was very different earlier than it is today.

After that

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//c17914f2-b0b6-4c95-94a1-cf69313c1ef0/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_91_389_409_641.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A50Z%2F-1%2F%2Fdd6cbcdc3177ca75d96b747ed52610ef10b3194de6c9551381d9a588817d8bab" alt="Image" width="26%" /></div>


Now

People travelled on horses.

### WORD MASTER

diversity-unlike

triotism-devotion towards our nation

freedom- to be free without other's control

unity- being together happily

seal-an official mark used for stamping

##### LET'S LEARN

C. Choose the correct option.

1. ___ is also known as Hindustan and India.

Bharat Bhutan Delhi

2. White colour in our flag is the symbol of ___.

○ truth ○ growth ○ both of these

3. Long ago people used to connect ___

☐ using mobiles ☐ by writing letters ☐ using video calling

4. Bara Imambara is located in _____

Delhi Mumbai Lucknow

2. List two things on which we can see our National Emblem.

#### LIFE SKILL- CELEBRATING DIVERSITY

You are at your friend's house. There, you are served food on a banana leaf. You are surprised as you always eat in a plate. What will you do?

(fi'l in the blanks)

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//b35e831f-833b-4d2c-a288-dba1c93ddbfc/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_823_613_1160_859.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A51Z%2F-1%2F%2F856fb991a66991a134b1d125780cd7e764505d0dfd09b7045e6ce6f8a2aba655" alt="Image" width="28%" /></div>


I will eat/not eat ___ that food.

I will ask/not ask ___ them to serve the food in a plate.

All families have their own culture. We should respect/disrespect ___

all cultures. We should also respect/disrespect ___ all food choices.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//b35e831f-833b-4d2c-a288-dba1c93ddbfc/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_235_1129_306_1296.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A51Z%2F-1%2F%2F2699ec76bdea4b8fa9ff81e3c9a081488855e5f772f0997d92e35493a7da1554" alt="Image" width="5%" /></div>


We should respect and celebrate diversity. This is the beauty of being an Indian.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//b35e831f-833b-4d2c-a288-dba1c93ddbfc/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_123_1299_335_1404.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A51Z%2F-1%2F%2F87a12b393c06559e2cb9a07c018172eeb7c2f19b91ca7c837e0fc7c1bb7774bc" alt="Image" width="17%" /></div>

# ANIMALS AROUND THE WORLD

Giraffes are found in Africa. They are the tallest living land animals.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//dde4373b-1212-432a-ba2c-d5a874159ff1/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_244_258_413_473.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A14%3A18Z%2F-1%2F%2F50c83ef48fab2b87487bb9f4b2e0d8b6133e761be4cfd0d5ebfdb600680e7a87" alt="Image" width="14%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//dde4373b-1212-432a-ba2c-d5a874159ff1/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_954_82_1115_377.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A14%3A18Z%2F-1%2F%2F34d23338612e94d6f944e7a6633a9819d8e2d421d9d8153e57518350b0bbd1f8" alt="Image" width="13%" /></div>


Giant pandas are found in Asia. They love eating bamboo

Polar bears live in Arctic region. They have black skin under their fur. They are very quick swimmers and love eating flesh of other animals.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//dde4373b-1212-432a-ba2c-d5a874159ff1/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_728_421_1136_732.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A14%3A18Z%2F-1%2F%2F5b77be0908dffa68bfc32514c84e079b2bb0b5e69e84e64ed727609ea1e40c7f" alt="Image" width="34%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//dde4373b-1212-432a-ba2c-d5a874159ff1/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_474_669_541_751.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A14%3A18Z%2F-1%2F%2F0a447cb8f37665897d20280a25338655b3274bd16e7d5ab966b2c8535be21618" alt="Image" width="5%" /></div>

Penguins are birds living in Antarctica. They cannot but are very good swimmers.

Kangaroos live in Australia. They can jump very high. Koalas also live in Australia. They love eating eucalyptus leaves.

Reindeers are found in Europe. They are from the des family.

Grizzly bears are found in North America. They need large spaces to live in.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//dde4373b-1212-432a-ba2c-d5a874159ff1/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_964_1306_1136_1504.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A14%3A18Z%2F-1%2F%2F5cd7c4c2a2bb659f506823d469a6927eac90d7047b64c667f2559cef8eaa8a89" alt="Image" width="14%" /></div>

##### LIFE SKILL- MAKING CONNECTIONS

A new girl, Diana came from an African country to your class. She does not know how to speak in Hindi or English. She wants to talk to everyone in the class. What good choice will you make to help her?

○ Talk to her using gestures.

○ Help her in learning our language.

Make fun of her with your friends.

Leave her alone.

The sky looks different during the day and at night.

We see many things in the sky like the Moon, clouds, stars and the Sun.

##### The Moon

We see the Moon at night. The shape of the Moon keeps changing. When the shape of the Moon is like a ball, we call it a full moon. At times, we cannot see the Moon at all. We call it a new moon.

Full moon

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d918472d-176b-43db-ac5f-050405eb7fad/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_193_518_1096_1006.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2Fd5fa405845957f7e426f4c5c0c8110c37f5f5381ad13497ea097c174cfeb2a70" alt="Image" width="75%" /></div>

##### Clouds

Clouds look like balls of cotton. They float in the sky. Clouds change their colours. Sometimes they are blue, while sometimes they are grey.

It usually rains when there are dark clouds in the sky.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d918472d-176b-43db-ac5f-050405eb7fad/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_813_1164_1071_1420.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A47Z%2F-1%2F%2F857622e87ff83e48244817c9d420e86082e456c8bcb625bca617d7d70cdb05a1" alt="Image" width="21%" /></div>


Dark clouds and Rain

Sometimes, after the rain, we see a band of seven colours across the sky. It is called a rainbow.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d918472d-176b-43db-ac5f-050405eb7fad/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_715_46_1127_280.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2F9857f06d5e2c59409c454968f53cd5d7ee27853ffcb664a592259693e49323f9" alt="Image" width="34%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d918472d-176b-43db-ac5f-050405eb7fad/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_11_295_165_438.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2Fc6b140fc3cc4314b997b6c1f651e5d327792c903f13023783a970ce9b1d47ed2" alt="Image" width="12%" /></div>

##### Stars

Stars twinkle in the sky at night. They are very big. They look so small because they are far away from us. There are so many stars in the sky that it is impossible to count them.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d918472d-176b-43db-ac5f-050405eb7fad/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_672_609_1116_917.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2Fdc21b5784efde2ac1f9ac5d9372b13cc657e73a5d6fd8b88ad8400028496aeea" alt="Image" width="37%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d918472d-176b-43db-ac5f-050405eb7fad/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_0_843_135_956.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2F05b5801ea3c2f188e7fd689e33cb58f6d98fde87e946dc5885b670a76c47707c" alt="Image" width="11%" /></div>


The Sun is also a star. Since it is close to us, it appears big to us. The Sun gives us heat and light. It is a big ball of fire. All living things need the warmth of the Sun to live. The Sun and the eight planets form the Solar System.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d918472d-176b-43db-ac5f-050405eb7fad/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_23_1112_1142_1546.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2Ff66c8c552fe2438440fe1b0bd3f0f952dad1cb0f990d796d3bc60e0720d500e7" alt="Image" width="94%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d918472d-176b-43db-ac5f-050405eb7fad/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_124_60_200_126.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2F29ba6b16f0e16f8b8b51803c01bac3781ce2555ea73e5ef5be1e83688681ed5e" alt="Image" width="6%" /></div>

##### OUR EARTH

Our earth is one of the planets of the Solar System. The Earth is the only known planet with air and water. So, we are able to live on the Earth.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d918472d-176b-43db-ac5f-050405eb7fad/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_916_418_1153_710.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2Fc6041fa0092b9fbb0997448caab5e23dd747865e0f6ddeeae764c70f8d27e40a" alt="Image" width="19%" /></div>


Most of the Earth is covered with water. The remaining part is land. The land has many forms like

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d918472d-176b-43db-ac5f-050405eb7fad/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_295_777_998_1231.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A48Z%2F-1%2F%2F33f7019e6f9c061a2b855250fb13b05f28dd26408351cbdfbb06ebc4e4f2e055" alt="Image" width="59%" /></div>


Plain- Land which is flat and smooth is called plain. Most of our crops grow on plains. Hill- Part of land which is higher than its surrounding land is called a hill. Apples, cherries, peaches and plums grow on hills.

Mountain- Very high hills are called mountains. Tops of the mountains are sometimes covered with snow.

Valley-The low lying land between two hills or mountains is called a valley. It is very beautiful and green.

Desert- Part of land covered with sand is called a desert. It is very hot in a desert. These places get little or no rainfall.

Forest- Part of land, where plants grow very close to one another is called a forest. Wild animals live in forests.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d918472d-176b-43db-ac5f-050405eb7fad/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_380_203_448_285.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A49Z%2F-1%2F%2F8cb37a839e249063630078fc5dc5ac62f0140afec35a1e2ee5d298ecac7615eb" alt="Image" width="5%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d918472d-176b-43db-ac5f-050405eb7fad/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_42_282_146_406.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A49Z%2F-1%2F%2F26a4d380be1f3d6f05794168862242b1a8442e87e20fdc4f62fbc03d1ad33cb8" alt="Image" width="8%" /></div>


##### WISDOM BOX

The Earth rotates on its axis. This movement causes day and night.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//d918472d-176b-43db-ac5f-050405eb7fad/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_988_245_1099_363.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A13%3A49Z%2F-1%2F%2F9c6f56bd4057731289eb33277ba87f89d5902080b97a1a5df4329f57cdde8964" alt="Image" width="9%" /></div>


##### LAND POLLUTION

Now a days, the land on the Earth is getting polluted. We dispose off wastes on land which is making it dirty.

##### Land pollution is caused by-

waste from our houses.

• growing more and more plants.

· proper disposal of wastes.

The above pictures show that Tanya is a _____ (kind/unkind) She is showing _____ (gratitude/ingratitude) by using magical words, like _____ and _____

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//b2a65b95-6b17-4bf9-9924-896025ba3069/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_22_1167_153_1330.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-16T02%3A14%3A11Z%2F-1%2F%2Fcd176e2c43936f81d74da5d44ec765541bc483e17c3b84778c402206c0ebb97e" alt="Image" width="11%" /></div>


Using magical words like- 'Please', 'Sorry' and 'Thank You' make us a good person. The one who uses these words gets love and respect from all.
